<script>
$(function() {
    $(".hd_pops_reject").click(function() {
        var id = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
        var ck_name = id[1];
        var exp_time = parseInt(id[2]);
        $("#"+id[1]).css("display", "none");
        
        var today = new Date();
        today.setTime(today.getTime() + (60*60*1000*exp_time));
        document.cookie = ck_name + "=" + escape( 1 ) + "; path=/; expires=" + today.toGMTString() + ";";
        if (g5_cookie_domain) {
            document.cookie += "domain=" + g5_cookie_domain + ";";
        }
    });
    $('.hd_pops_close').click(function() {
        var idb = $(this).attr('class').split(' ');
        $('#'+idb[1]).css('display','none');
    });
    $("#hd").css("z-index", 1000);
});
</script>

	function SetUser(id){
		if (id==1){
			$("#member").show();
			$("#login").css("bottom","300px").animate({"bottom":"0px"},300).show();	
			$("#join").hide();
		}else if (id==2){
			$("#member").show();
			$("#join").css("bottom","300px").animate({"bottom":"0px"},300).show();	
			$("#login").hide();
		}
	}		
	function Setclose(){	
			$("#member").hide();
			$("#login").hide();
			$("#join").hide();
	}

			<script>
            function fsearchbox_submit(f)
            {
                if (f.stx.value.length < 2) {
                    alert("검색어는 두글자 이상 입력하십시오.");
                    f.stx.select();
                    f.stx.focus();
                    return false;
                }

                // 검색에 많은 부하가 걸리는 경우 이 주석을 제거하세요.
                var cnt = 0;
                for (var i=0; i<f.stx.value.length; i++) {
                    if (f.stx.value.charAt(i) == ' ')
                        cnt++;
                }

                if (cnt > 1) {
                    alert("빠른 검색을 위하여 검색어에 공백은 한개만 입력할 수 있습니다.");
                    f.stx.select();
                    f.stx.focus();
                    return false;
                }

                return true;
            }
            </script>
        </ul>

	<script type="text/javascript">/*
 * Very simple jQuery Color Picker
 * https://github.com/tkrotoff/jquery-simplecolorpicker
 *
 * Copyright (C) 2012-2013 Tanguy Krotoff <tkrotoff@gmail.com>
 *
 * Licensed under the MIT license
 */

(function($) {
  'use strict';

  /**
   * Constructor.
   */
  var SimpleColorPicker = function(select, options) {
    this.init('simplecolorpicker', select, options);
  };

  /**
   * SimpleColorPicker class.
   */
  SimpleColorPicker.prototype = {
    constructor: SimpleColorPicker,

    init: function(type, select, options) {
      var self = this;

      self.type = type;

      self.$select = $(select);
      self.$select.hide();

      self.options = $.extend({}, $.fn.simplecolorpicker.defaults, options);

      self.$colorList = null;

      if (self.options.picker === true) {
        var selectText = self.$select.find('> option:selected').text();
        self.$icon = $('<span class="simplecolorpicker icon"'
  //                   + ' title="' + selectText + '"'
                     + ' style="background-color: ' + self.$select.val() + ';"'
                     + ' role="button" tabindex="0">'
                     + '</span>').insertAfter(self.$select);
        self.$icon.on('click.' + self.type, $.proxy(self.showPicker, self));

        self.$picker = $('<span class="simplecolorpicker picker ' + self.options.theme + '"></span>').appendTo(document.body);
        self.$colorList = self.$picker;

        // Hide picker when clicking outside
        $(document).on('mousedown.' + self.type, $.proxy(self.hidePicker, self));
        self.$picker.on('mousedown.' + self.type, $.proxy(self.mousedown, self));
      } else {
        self.$inline = $('<span class="simplecolorpicker inline ' + self.options.theme + '"></span>').insertAfter(self.$select);
        self.$colorList = self.$inline;
      }
      
      
	  self.$picker.css({
	      display: 'inline-block',
	      maxWidth: $('body').width() < 300 ? $('body').width() - 15 : 300
	  });

      // Build the list of colors
      // <span class="color selected" title="Green" style="background-color: #7bd148;" role="button"></span>
      self.$select.find('> option').each(function() {
        var $option = $(this);
        var color = $option.val();

        var isSelected = $option.is(':selected');
        var isDisabled = $option.is(':disabled');

        var selected = '';
        if (isSelected === true) {
          selected = ' data-selected';
        }

        var disabled = '';
        if (isDisabled === true) {
          disabled = ' data-disabled';
        }
/*
        var title = '';
        if (isDisabled === false) {
          title = ' title="' + $option.text() + '"';
        }
*/
        var role = '';
        if (isDisabled === false) {
          role = ' role="button" tabindex="0"';
        }

        var $colorSpan = $('<span class="color"'
                         //+ title
                         + ' style="background-color: ' + color + ';"'
                         + ' data-color="' + color + '"'
                         + selected
                         + disabled
                         + role + '>'
                         + '</span>');

        self.$colorList.append($colorSpan);
        $colorSpan.on('click.' + self.type, $.proxy(self.colorSpanClicked, self));

        var $next = $option.next();
        if ($next.is('optgroup') === true) {
          // Vertical break, like hr
          self.$colorList.append('<span class="vr"></span>');
        }
      });
    },

    /**
     * Changes the selected color.
     *
     * @param color the hexadecimal color to select, ex: '#fbd75b'
     */
    selectColor: function(color) {
      var self = this;

      var $colorSpan = self.$colorList.find('> span.color').filter(function() {
        return $(this).data('color').toLowerCase() === color.toLowerCase();
      });

      if ($colorSpan.length > 0) {
        self.selectColorSpan($colorSpan);
      } else {
        console.error("The given color '" + color + "' could not be found");
      }
    },

    showPicker: function(e) {
      var pos = this.$icon.offset();
	  var x = pos.left;
	  if(x > $('body').width() - this.$colorList.outerWidth() + 15) 
		  x = $('body').width() - this.$colorList.outerWidth();
      this.$picker.css({
        // Remove some pixels to align the picker icon with the icons inside the dropdown
        left: x,
        top: pos.top - this.$colorList.outerHeight()
      });

      this.$picker.show(this.options.pickerDelay);
    },

    hidePicker: function() {
      this.$picker.hide(this.options.pickerDelay);
    },

    /**
     * Selects the given span inside $colorList.
     *
     * The given span becomes the selected one.
     * It also changes the HTML select value, this will emit the 'change' event.
     */
    selectColorSpan: function($colorSpan) {
      var color = $colorSpan.data('color');
      //var title = $colorSpan.prop('title');

      // Mark this span as the selected one
      $colorSpan.siblings().removeAttr('data-selected');
      $colorSpan.attr('data-selected', '');

      if (this.options.picker === true) {
        this.$icon.css('background-color', color);
        //this.$icon.prop('title', title);
        //this.hidePicker();,
      }

      // Change HTML select value
      this.$select.val(color);
    },

    /**
     * The user clicked on a color inside $colorList.
     */
    colorSpanClicked: function(e) {
      // When a color is clicked, make it the new selected one (unless disabled)
      if ($(e.target).is('[data-disabled]') === false) {
        this.selectColorSpan($(e.target));
        this.$select.trigger('change');
      }
    },

    /**
     * Prevents the mousedown event from "eating" the click event.
     */
    mousedown: function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.preventDefault();
    },

    destroy: function() {
      if (this.options.picker === true) {
        this.$icon.off('.' + this.type);
        this.$icon.remove();
        $(document).off('.' + this.type);
      }

      this.$colorList.off('.' + this.type);
      this.$colorList.remove();

      this.$select.removeData(this.type);
      this.$select.show();
    }
  };

  /**
   * Plugin definition.
   * How to use: $('#id').simplecolorpicker()
   */
  $.fn.simplecolorpicker = function(option) {
    var args = $.makeArray(arguments);
    args.shift();

    // For HTML element passed to the plugin
    return this.each(function() {
      var $this = $(this),
        data = $this.data('simplecolorpicker'),
        options = typeof option === 'object' && option;
      if (data === undefined) {
        $this.data('simplecolorpicker', (data = new SimpleColorPicker(this, options)));
      }
      if (typeof option === 'string') {
        data[option].apply(data, args);
      }
    });
  };

  /**
   * Default options.
   */
  $.fn.simplecolorpicker.defaults = {
    // No theme by default
    theme: '',

    // Show the picker or make it inline
    picker: false,

    // Animation delay in milliseconds
    pickerDelay: 0
  };

})(jQuery);</script>
	
	<script type="text/javascript">function popup_module() {
	var now = undefined;
	var list = [];
	var self = this;
	var count = 0;
	//pb.css({ 'opacity' : 0.4 });
	$(function() {
		self.html = $('#popup_frame').html();
		self.pb = $('#popupBackground');
		self.pu = $('#popupWrap');
	})
	this.add = function (html, type, funx, after) {
		count++;
		list.push({html : html, type: type, fun:funx, after:after, code:count});
		on();
		return count;
	}
	this.confirm = function(title, subtitle, fn) {
		var dom = $(this.html);
		return this.add(dom, 'confirm', function(layer, pb, pu) {
			var $this = this;
			pu.find('.title').text(title);
			pu.find('dt').text(subtitle);
			layer.centering();
			pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(true);
			}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(false);
			});
			pb.one('click', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			}); 
		});


	}
	this.prompt = function(title, subtitle, value, fn) {
		var dom = $(this.html);
		return this.add(dom, 'prompt', function(layer, pb, pu) {
			var $this = this;
			pu.find('.title').text(title);
			pu.find('dt').text(subtitle);
			pu.find('dd').append('<input class="prompt_data"/>');
			pu.find('input:first').val(value).focus();
			layer.centering();

			pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
				var result = pu.find(".prompt_data").val();
				layer.close();
				fn(result);
			}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			});
			pb.one('click', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			}); 
		});
	}
	this.password = function( title, subtitle, value, fn) {
		var dom = $(this.html);
		return this.add(dom, 'password', function(layer, pb, pu) {
			var $this = this;
			pu.find('.title').text(title);
			pu.find('dt').text(subtitle);
			pu.find('dd').append('<input type="password" class="prompt_data"/>');
			pu.find('input:first').val(value).focus();
			layer.centering();

			pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
				var result = pu.find(".prompt_data").val();
				layer.close();
				fn(result);
			}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			});
			pb.one('click', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			}); 
		});
	}
	this.alert = function(title, content, fn, after) {
		var dom = $(this.html);
		return this.add(dom, 'alert', function(layer, pb, pu) {
			pu.find('.title').text(title);
			pu.find('.content').html(content);
			pu.find('.cancel').hide();

			layer.centering();
			pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
				layer.close();
			});
			pb.one('click', function() {
				layer.close();
			});
			fn && fn(layer, pb, pu);
		}, after);
	}
	this.select = function(title, subtitle, list, fn) {
		var dom = $(this.html);
		return this.add(dom, 'select', function(layer, pb, pu) {
			pu.find('.title').text(title);
			pu.find('dt').text(subtitle);
			var select = $('<select class="select_data" />');
			for(var i in list) {
				select.append($('<option />').val(i).text(list[i]));
			}
			pu.find('dd').append(select);
			layer.centering();

			pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
				var result = pu.find(".select_data").val();
				layer.close();
				fn(result);
			}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			});
			pb.one('click', function() {
				layer.close();
				fn(null);
			}); 
		});
	}
	function on () {
		if(now)
			return;
		if(!list[0])
			return;
		now = list.shift();
		self.pu.off('.pop_btn');
		self.pu.on('keypress', function(e) {
			if(e.keyCode == 13)
				self.pu.find('.ok').click();
			//return false;
		});
		if(typeof now.html === 'string') {
			self.pu.html(now.html);
		} else {
			self.pu.html('');
			self.pu.append(now.html);
		}
		self.pu.show();
		self.pb.show();
		self.pu.width(self.pu.children().outerWidth(true)).height(self.pu.children().outerHeight(true));
		puCenter();
		now.fun({close: returnCallback(now.code), centering : puCenter }, self.pb, self.pu);
	}

	function returnCallback (code) { 
		return function() {
			self.close(code);
		}
	}

	this.close = function(id) {
		if(typeof id !== 'undefined') {
			if(now && now.code == id) {
				this.close();
			} else {
				for (var i=list.length-1, l=0; i>=l; i--) {
					if(list[i].code == id){ 
						list.splice(i, 1);
					}
				} 
			}
		} else {
			self.pu.off().hide();
			self.pb.off().hide();
			self.pu.empty();

			if(now) {
				if(typeof now.after == 'function') {
					try {
						now.after();
					} catch(e) {
						console.error(e);
					}
				}
			}
			now = undefined;
			on();
		}
	}
	this.closeByType = function(target) {
		if(target) { 
			for(var i=list.length-1, l=0; i>=l; i--) {
				if(list[i].type == target){ 
					this.close(list[i].code);
				}
			}
			if(now && now.type == target)
				this.close();
		}
	}

	function puCenter() {
		self.pu.width('auto').css({'left':$('body').width()/2-self.pu.outerWidth()/2+'px', 'top':$('body').height()/2-self.pu.outerHeight()/2+'px' });
	}
}	
</script>

function top_layer_module(target) {
	this.target = target;
	this.init_top = target.offset().top;
	this.init_left = target.offset().left;
	this.layer_floor = $('#top_layer_floor').html();
	this.layer_wrap = $('#top_layer_wrap').html();

	this.init = function() {
		this.wrap = $(this.layer_wrap);
		target.parent().css('position', 'relative').append(this.wrap);
		return this;
	}
	this.add = function(text, bgcolor, ftcolor, timeout, link, weight) {
		var floor = $(this.layer_floor);
		bgcolor && floor.css('backgroundColor', bgcolor);
		ftcolor && floor.css('color', ftcolor);
		floor.find('.text').text(text);
		floor.find('.close').click(function() {
			floor.remove();
		});
		floor.data('weight', weight);
		if(timeout && timeout < 0x7FFFFFFF) { 
			setTimeout(function() { 
				floor.remove();
			}, timeout);
		}
		if(link) {
			floor.find('.text').append('<div class="iconLink"></div>');
			floor.css('cursor', 'pointer').click(function() {
				if(link.indexOf('javascript:') === 0)
					top.location.href = link;
				else
					window.open(link);
			});
		}
		var wrote = false;
		this.wrap.find('.floor').each(function(index) {
			if($(this).data('weight') < floor.data('weight')) {
				wrote = true;
				$(this).before(floor);
				return false;
			}
		});
		if(!wrote) {
			this.wrap.append(floor);
		}
		floor.addClass(isWhiteness(floor.css('backgroundColor'))?'black':'white');
		return floor;
	}
	this.remove = function() {
		this.wrap.html('');
	}
}

function whisper_module(stage) {
	var target = '';

	this.getTarget = function () {
		return target;
	}
	this.get = function() {
		if(target)
			return '/w '+target+' ';
		else
			return '';
	}
	this.add = function ( nickname ) {
		if(!nickname)
			return;
		target = nickname;
		var html = '';
		html += '<div class="target nick" nick="'+escape(nickname)+'"><span>'+text(nickname)+'</span>&nbsp;<span class="cancle">x</span></div>';
		stage.html(html);
	}
	this.remove = function () {
		target = '';
		stage.html('');
		return false;
	}
	stage.on('click', '.cancle', this.remove);
}

function commandSwitch(room, arr) {
	var command = arr.shift().toLowerCase();
	switch(command) {
		case 'w':
		case 'ㅈ':
			whisper.add(arr.shift());
			room.action.command('whisper', whisper.getTarget(), arr.join(' '));
			break;
		case 'r':
		case 'ㄱ':
			whisper.add(rooms[room.id].log.last_whisper);
			room.action.command('whisper', whisper.getTarget(), arr.join(' '));
			break;
		case 'ban':
			var target = arr.shift();
			var reason = arr.join(' ');
			if(!reason)
				popup.prompt('차단', '사유', '', function(reason) {
					if(reason === null)
						return;
					room.action.command('ban', target, reason);
				});
			break;
		case 'report':
			var target = arr.shift();
			var reason = arr.join(' ');
			if(!reason)
				popup.prompt('신고', '사유', '', function(reason) {
					if(reason === null)
						return;
					room.action.command('report', target, reason);
				});
			break;
		case 'upload':
			room.action.command('upload', function(upload_json) {
				if(upload_json.status)
					$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).append(upload_json.url);
				else
					alert(upload_json.msg);
			});
			break;
		case 'mute':
			var target = arr.shift();
			popup.prompt('채팅금지', '시간(분)', '5', function(time) {
				if(time === null)
					return;
				room.action.command('mute', target, time);
			});
			break;
		case 'unmute':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command('unmute', target);
			break;
		case 'call':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command('call', target);
			break;
		case 'ip':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command('ip', target);
			break;
		case 'popup':
			room.action.command('popup');
			break;
		case 'individual':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command('invite', target);
			break;
		case 'ignore':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command("ignore", target);
			break;
		case 'un_ignore':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command("un_ignore", target);
			break;
		case '닉네임':
		case 'nick':
		case '닉':
			var nickname = arr.shift();
			room.action.command("changeInfo", {"nick": nickname});
			break;
		case 'op':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command("op", target);
			break;
		case 'deop':
			var target = arr.shift();
			room.action.command("deop", target);
			break;
		case 'myinfo':
			$('.my_information', rooms[room.id].layout).click();
			break;
		case 'login':
			var password = arr.shift();
			room.action.command('login', password);
			break;
		case 'frozen':
			room.action.command('frozen');
			break;
		
		case 'defrozen':
			room.action.command('defrozen');
			break;
		case 'logout':
			room.action.command('logout');
			break;
		case 'test':
			popup.select('테스트', '내용', {'dlfma':1, '두번째':2}, function(data) { 
				alert(data);
			});
			break;
		default:
			room.action.command.apply(undefined, [command].concat(arr));
			//room.action.command(command);


	};
}
function filter_character(data) {
    if(isArray(data)) {
        for(var i = 0, limit = data.length; i<limit; i++ ) {
            if(isStr(data[i]))
                data[i] = filter_character(data[i]);
        }
        return data;
    } else if(isStr(data)) {
		data2 = data.replace(printable_regex, '');
		for(var i = 0, l = data2.length; i<l; i++) {
			data = data.replace(data2[i], '\ufffd');
		}
		return data;
    } else
        return data;
}

function remove_multi_space(msg) {
	if(isArray(msg)) {
		for(var i = 0, limit = msg.length; i<limit; i++) {
			if(isStr(msg[i])) {
				msg[i] = remove_multi_space(msg[i]);
			}
		}
		return msg;
	} else if (isStr(msg)) {
		return msg.replace(/\s\s+/g, ' ');
	} else 
		return msg;

}

function text(data) {
	return remove_multi_space(filter_character(escapeHTML(data)));
}

$(function() { // 전체 채팅방에 대한 공통적인 사항
	
	// Tooltip only Text
	tooltip = $('.tooltip');
	var tipTimer = 0;
	var x = 0;
	$('body').on('mouseover', '[title], [data-tiptext]', function(e){
		var self = $(this);
		clearTimeout(tipTimer);
		x = e.pageX;
		tipTimer = setTimeout(function() {
			// Hover over code
			var title = unescape(self.attr('title') || self.attr('data-tiptext'));
			self.removeAttr('title').attr('data-tiptext', title);
			if(self.attr('created')) 
				title = title.replace('{ago}', timeSince(Uchat.getServerSecond(), self.attr('created')*1000));
			tooltip.text(title);

			var y = self.offset().top - tooltip.outerHeight(true) - 3;
			var now_x = x - tooltip.outerWidth(true)/2; //$(this).offset().left + $(this).outerWidth()/2 - tooltip.outerWidth(true)/2;

			if( now_x < 0 )
				now_x = 0;
			if( now_x > $('body').width() - tooltip.outerWidth())
				now_x = $('body').width() - tooltip.outerWidth();

			if( y < 0 )
				y = self.offset().top + self.outerHeight() + 3;
			if( y > $('body').height() - tooltip.outerHeight())
				y = $('body').height() - tooltip.outerHeight();

			tooltip.css({ top: y +7 , left: now_x });
			tooltip.animate({top: y}, 'fast').fadeIn({queue: false, duration:'normal'});

			clearTimeout(tipTimer);
		}, 400);
	}).on('mouseleave', '[title], [data-tiptext]', function() {
		// Hover out code
		//$(this).attr('title', $(this).data('tipText'));
		tooltip.stop().fadeOut('fast');
		clearTimeout(tipTimer);
	}).on('mousemove', '[title], [data-tiptext]', function(e) { 
		x = e.pageX;
	});
	$(document).mouseleave(function() {
		clearTimeout(tipTimer); // 밖에 나갔는데 뜨면 안됨
		tooltip.stop().hide();
	});
});


function layout_init(room) {
	//room.nano = $('.nano', rooms[room.id].layout).nanoScroller();
	
	room.skin.dom = rooms[room.id].dom = {};
	rooms[room.id].dom.wrap = $('.wrap', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.top = $('.top', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.menubar = $('.menuBar', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.bottom = $('.bottom', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.setting = $('.settingContent', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.settingBG = $('.settingBackground', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.latest_chat = $('.latest_chat', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.chatInputHidden = $('.chatInputHidden', rooms[room.id].layout);

	rooms[room.id].dom.userList = $('.userListWrap', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.content = $('.contentWrap', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.contour = $('.contour', rooms[room.id].layout);
	rooms[room.id].dom.content_target = $('.content', rooms[room.id].layout).not(".scroll-wrapper");

	room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor = room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor || '#ffffff';
	room.skin.arguments.topBGColor = room.skin.arguments.topBGColor || shadeColor2(room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor, isWhiteness(room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor)?-0.045:-0.07);
	room.skin.arguments.middleBGColor = room.skin.arguments.middleBGColor || room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor;
	room.skin.arguments.bottomBGColor = room.skin.arguments.bottomBGColor || room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor;
	room.skin.arguments.settingBGColor = room.skin.arguments.settingBGColor || room.skin.arguments.defaultBGColor;

	rooms[room.id].dom.top.css('backgroundColor', room.skin.arguments.topBGColor).addClass(isWhiteness(room.skin.arguments.topBGColor)?'black':'white');

		}
		*/
	}
	rooms[room.id].userListDom = (function() {
		var middle = rooms[room.id].dom.middle, dom = rooms[room.id].dom.userList;

		function show() {
			room.action.command('userList');
			room.action.command('io', true);
			dom.show();
		}
		function hide() {
			room.action.command('io', false);
			dom.hide();
			dom.find('.userFloor').remove();
		}
		function resize() {
			if(middle.is('.vertical'))
				rooms[room.id].dom.content.height(rooms[room.id].dom.middle.height() - rooms[room.id].dom.contour.outerHeight(true) - rooms[room.id].dom.userList.filter(':visible').outerHeight(true));
			else
				rooms[room.id].dom.content.width(parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.middle[0].getBoundingClientRect().width) - rooms[room.id].dom.contour.outerWidth(true) - rooms[room.id].dom.userList.filter(':visible').outerWidth(true));
			room.skin.scrollDown();
		}
		function toggle() {
			if(dom.is(':visible') || room.skin.arguments.nerverOpenUserList)
				hide();
			else
				show();
			resize();
		}
		function init() {
			if (room.skin.arguments.hideUserList || !room.info.io || room.skin.arguments.nerverOpenUserList || (rooms[room.id].dom.middle.hasClass("horizontal") && rooms[room.id].dom.middle.width() <= 397) || (rooms[room.id].dom.middle.hasClass('vertical') && rooms[room.id].dom.middle.height() < 270) )
				hide(); // io 안보내기 위해 직접 컨트롤
			else
				show();
			resize();
		}
		return {
			dom: dom
				, init: init
				, show: show
				, hide: hide

		//rooms[room.id].menubar.add('scroll', $('#scroll').html());

		$(window).resize(function (event, room_id) {

			var wrap_height = $('body').height()
					- parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.css('borderTopWidth'))
					- parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.css('borderBottomWidth'))
					- parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.css('paddingTop'))

			(function (shape) {

				switch (shape) {

						rooms[room.id].dom.content.width('auto').height(rooms[room.id].dom.middle.height() - rooms[room.id].dom.contour.outerHeight(true) - rooms[room.id].dom.userList.filter(':visible').outerHeight(true));
						break;

						rooms[room.id].dom.middle.removeClass('vertical').addClass('horizontal');
						rooms[room.id].dom.userList.height('100%').width(rooms[room.id].dom.userList.data('width') || room.skin.arguments.userListWidth || 150);
						rooms[room.id].dom.content.height('100%').width(parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.middle[0].getBoundingClientRect().width) - rooms[room.id].dom.contour.outerWidth(true) - rooms[room.id].dom.userList.filter(':visible').outerWidth(true));
						break;
					default:
						if ($(window).height() > $(window).width())
							arguments.callee(1);
						else
							arguments.callee(2);
						break;
				}
			})();

			//$('.plusWrap', rooms[room.id].layout).css({bottom:$('.bottom', rooms[room.id].layout).outerHeight(true) + parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.css('borderBottomWidth')) + parseInt(rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.css('paddingBottom'))});
			/*
				shape 에 따라 스타일 변경.
				0 : 자동 ( 높이가 넓이보다 크면 세로형, 아니면 가로형)
				1 : 세로형
				2 : 가로형
			*/
			//$('.content', rooms[room.id].layout).not(".scroll-wrapper").append('<p>'+$(window).height()+'</p>');
			room.skin.scrollDown(true);
		}).resize();
		rooms[room.id].dom.content.on('mouseover', 'a', function(e) {
			var href = $(this).attr('href'), image_url = '';
			if(href && href.match(/\.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif)$/gi))
				image_url = href;
			else if (href && href.match(/^(https?)?:?\/\/(\w+\.)?imgur.com\/(\w*\d\w*)+(\.[a-zA-Z]{3})?$/))
				image_url = href+'.jpg';
			else if(href.match(/youtu(be\.com|\.be)(\/\watch\?v\=|\/embed\/|\/)(.{11})/))
				image_url = '//img.youtube.com/vi/'+href.match(/youtu(be\.com|\.be)(\/\watch\?v=|\/embed\/|\/)(.{11})/).pop()+'/0.jpg';

			if(image_url) {
				popup.add('<div style="width:200px; text-align:center;"><img src="'+image_url+'" style="max-width:200px; max-height:200px;vertical-align:bottom"></div>', 'imageView', function(layer, pb, pu) {
					pb.hide();
					var x = $(e.target).offset().left + $(e.target).width()/2 -100;
					var y = $(e.target).offset().top-pu.find('img').height()-10;
					/*
					if($('body').height()/2 > $(this).offset().top) {
						y = $(this).offset().top - 5;
					} else {
						y = $(this).offset().top
					}
					*/
					if(x<0)
						x = 0;
					if(y<0) {
						y = $(e.target).offset().top + $(e.target).height()+10;
						pu.find('>div').css('lineHeight', 1);
						pu.one('mouseleave', function(e) {
							layer.close();
						});
					}
					pu.css("top", y).css("left", x);
					if(pu.find('img').width() > 200 || pu.find('img').height() > 200) {
						if(pu.find('img').width() > pu.find('img').height())
							pu.find('img').width(200);
						else
							pu.find('img').height(200);
					}
					/*
					pb.one('mousemove', function() {
						layer.close();
					});
					*/
					/*
					pu.one('click', '.floor', function(event) {
						var target = pu.find('.subject').attr('nick');
						var kind = $(this).attr('kind');
						switch(kind) {
							case 'whisper':
								whisper.add(unescape(target));
								$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).focus();
								break;
							default:
								commandSwitch(room, [kind, unescape(target)]);
								break;

						}
						layer.close();
					});*/
				});
			}
		}).on('mouseleave', 'a', function(e) {

		rooms[room.id].dom.middle.on('mousedown', '.contour', function(e) {
			var b = rooms[room.id].dom.middle, c = rooms[room.id].dom.userList, d = $('.contentWrap', rooms[room.id].layout);
			$(this).addClass('draggable').parents().on('mousemove', function(e) {
				if(!rooms[room.id].dom.userList.is(':visible')) return false;
				var a = b.find('.draggable');
				if (b.is('.vertical')) {
					//console.log(c.offset()['top'], e.pageY, $('.draggable').outerHeight());
					if(a.length) {
						var cHeight = e.pageY - c.offset()['top'] - parseInt(a.outerHeight(true)/2), dHeight = b.height() - a.outerHeight(true) - cHeight;
						if(dHeight >= 0) {
							c.height(cHeight);
							c.data('height', cHeight);
							d.height(dHeight);
							room.skin.scrollDown(true);
						}
						//$(window).trigger('resize', [room_id]);
					}
				} else {
					//console.log(c.offset()['top'], e.pageY, $('.draggable').outerHeight());
					if(a.length) {
						var dWidth = e.pageX - d.offset()['left'] - parseInt(a.outerWidth(true)/2), cWidth = b.width() - a.outerWidth(true) - dWidth;
						//console.log(dWidth);
						if(dWidth >= 0 && cWidth >= 0) {
							c.width(cWidth);
							c.data('width', cWidth);
							d.width(dWidth);
						}
						//$(window).trigger('resize', [room_id]);
					}
				}
				a.addClass('moved');
			});
			e.preventDefault();
		});

		$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).keydown(function (event) {
			if (event.keyCode == 8) {
				if (!$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).text())
					whisper.remove();
			} else if (event.keyCode == 9) {
				whisper.add(rooms[room.id].log.last_whisper);
				$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).focus();
				return false;
			} else if (event.keyCode == 13) {
				if(room.agent.ios) {
					//$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).attr('readonly', true);
					//$(this).blur();
					send();
					var $this = this;
					//setTimeout(function() { $($this)[0].innerHTML = ''; });
					$(this).html('');
					//$(this).click();
					//$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).attr('readonly', false);
					//$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).focus();
				} else {
					send();
					$(this).html('');
					return false;

				}
				//$(this).html('');

				/*
				if (!room.agent.ios)
					return false;
				*/
			}
		}).keydown(function(event) {
			if(event.keyCode == 38) {
				if(rooms[room.id].log.now_chat == 9)
					return;
				if(rooms[room.id].log.chat[rooms[room.id].log.now_chat+1])
					$(this).text(rooms[room.id].log.chat[++rooms[room.id].log.now_chat]);
					placeCaretAtEnd($(this)[0]);
				return false;
			} else if(event.keyCode == 40) {
				if(rooms[room.id].log.now_chat == -1)
					return;
				if(rooms[room.id].log.chat[rooms[room.id].log.now_chat-1] || rooms[room.id].log.now_chat == 0) {
					$(this).text(rooms[room.id].log.chat[--rooms[room.id].log.now_chat]?rooms[room.id].log.chat[rooms[room.id].log.now_chat]:'');
					placeCaretAtEnd($(this)[0]);
				}
				return false;
			}
		}).keyup(function(date) {
			rooms[room.id].textarea_reload();
		});

		function send() {
			var text = strip($('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).html());
			if(!text) return false;
			text = whisper.get() + text;
			
			rooms[room.id].log.temp_scroll_stop = 0;
			room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] = 1;
			
			rooms[room.id].log.chat.unshift(text);
			if(rooms[room.id].log.chat.length > 10)
				rooms[room.id].log.chat.pop();
			rooms[room.id].log.now_chat = -1;

			if (command_regex.exec(text)) {
				text2 = text.replace(/^\//, '');
				var arr = text2.split(/\s/g);
				commandSwitch(room, arr);
				return true;
			} else if ( plugin_regex.exec(text) ) {
				text2 = text.replace(/^!/, '');
				var arr = text2.split(/\s/g);
				if(room.action.plugin(arr.shift(), arr) === true)
					return true;

			}
			var style =  {
					bold: room.setting.data['style.bold']
					, italic: room.setting.data['style.italic'] 
					, underline: room.setting.data['style.underline']
					, color: $('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).css('color')
			};
			room.action.send(text, style);

			room.skin.scrollDown();
		}

		function initSetting() {

				$('.settingContent .onlyadmin', rooms[room.id].layout).show();

			});
			*/
		}

				initSetting();

				rooms[room.id].dom.setting.css({top: e.pageY + 10, left:e.pageX - rooms[room.id].dom.setting.outerWidth(true), 'maxHeight': rooms[room.id].dom.wrap.height()-e.pageY-20});

				switch($(this).attr('kind')) {
					case 'frozen':
						if( !$(this).find('input[type=checkbox]').is(':checked') ) // 클릭하는 순간에는 변경되기 전이므로 반대로 한다.
							commandSwitch( room, [ 'frozen' ] );
						else
							commandSwitch( room, [ 'defrozen' ] );
						break;
					case 'clearLog':
						commandSwitch( room, [ 'clearLog' ] );
						break;
					default:
						room.setting.data[$(this).attr('kind')] = $(this).find('input[type=checkbox]').is(':checked')?0:1;  // 클릭하는 순간에는 변경되기 전이므로 반대로 한다.
						room.setting.save();
				}
			}
			//e.stopPropagation(); e.preventDefault();
		});

				*/

				var x = event.pageX;
				var y = event.pageY;

				/* ie7 에서 wrap 의 넓이가 안정해지면 자식객체가 width 를 100% 으로 써버림 (float:right 하는순간 width 100%)
				if(pu.outerWidth() < 120)
					pu.width(120);
					*/
				pu.width($('body').width() < 200? $('body').width():200);
				if( x < 0 )
					x = 0;
				if( x > $('body').width() - pu.outerWidth())
					x = $('body').width() - pu.outerWidth();
				if( y > $('body').height() - pu.outerHeight())
					y = $('body').height() - pu.outerHeight();
				pu.css("top", y).css("left", x);
				
				var html = '';

				for(var i =1; i <= 127; i++) {
					html += '<img src="//emoticon.inde.biz/emoticon/onionhead/'+leadingZeros(i, 3)+'.gif" code="onionhead|'+leadingZeros(i, 3)+'.gif">';
				}

				pu.find('.emoticon_middle').html(html);
				pb.on('click', function() {
					layer.close();
				});
				pu.on('click', 'img', function() {
					$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).append('<img src="'+$(this).attr('src')+'">');
					var el = $('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout)[0];
					el.focus();
					if (typeof window.getSelection != "undefined"
							&& typeof document.createRange != "undefined") {
						var range = document.createRange();
						range.selectNodeContents(el);
						range.collapse(false);
						var sel = window.getSelection();
						sel.removeAllRanges();
						sel.addRange(range);
					} else if (typeof document.body.createTextRange != "undefined") {
						var textRange = document.body.createTextRange();
						textRange.moveToElementText(el);
						textRange.collapse(false);
						textRange.select();
					}
					rooms[room.id].textarea_reload();
					layer.close();

				});
				/*
				pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
					//alert('오케이');

					layer.close();
					hideSetting();
				}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
					//alert('거절');
					layer.close();
					hideSetting();
				});
				*/
			});
		});
	});

}


function allot(str, data) {
	for( var i in data ) {
		if (!data.hasOwnProperty(i) || typeof(data[i]) === 'undefined') {
			continue;
		}
		str = str.replace(new RegExp("{"+i+"}", "gi"), data[i].replace("'", '&#39;').replace('"', '&quot;'));
	}
	return str;
}

function allot2(str, data) {
	if(!str)
		return '';
	for(var i in data) {
		str = str.replace('{'+i+'}', data[i]);
	}
	return str;
}
function imageMaker ( data, alt ) {
	var result = '';
	if(data)
		result = '<img src="'+data+'"'+(alt?' alt="'+(alt.replace(/"/gi, '&quot;'))+'"':'')+'>';
	return result;
}

function icons_parsing(data) {
	var icon_set = data.split('@');
	var icons_front_arr = (icon_set[0]||'').split(','); // 닉콘 앞 아이콘들
	var icons_back_arr = (icon_set[1]||'').split(','); // 닉콘 뒤 아이콘들
	var icons_front = '';
	var icons_back = '';
	for(var i = 0; i<icons_front_arr.length; i++)
		if(icons_front_arr[i])
			icons_front += imageMaker(icons_front_arr[i])+'&nbsp;';

	for(var i = 0; i<icons_back_arr.length; i++) {
		if(icons_back_arr[i])
			icons_back += '&nbsp;'+imageMaker(icons_back_arr[i]);
	}
	return [icons_front, icons_back];
}

function userFloorMaker( data ) {
	var html = '';
	var auth = '';
	var title = '';
	var addClass = '';
	switch(data['auth']) {
		case 3:
			title = ' <img src="//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/crown-icon.gif">';
			break;
		case 2:
			title = ' <img src="//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/crown-icon-s.gif">';
			break;
		case 1:
			title = '';
			break;
		case 0:
			title = '';
			break;
	}

	if(data['mute'])
		addClass += 'mute';

	var icon_set = icons_parsing(data['icons']);

	if(data['nickcon']) {
		var nickcon = imageMaker(data['nickcon'], data['nick']);
	}

	var html = ["<div class='userFloor nick ", addClass, "' nick='", escape(data['nick']), "' title='", text(data['nick']).replace(/'/gi, '&#39;'), " - {ago}", "' created='", data['time'], "'>", icon_set[0], "<span>", nickcon?nickcon:text(data['nick']), "</span>", icon_set[1], title, '</div>'];

	return html.join('');
}

function userFloorSend(room, html, data ) {
	var auth = 0;
	switch(data['auth']) {
		case 3:
			auth = 'admin';
			break;
		case 2:
			auth = 'subadmin';
			break;
		case 1:
			auth = 'member';
			break;
		case 0:
			auth = 'guest';
			break;
	}
	if(room.my.nick == data['nick'])
		$('.userList .i', rooms[room.id].layout).html(html);
	else
		$('.userList .'+auth+'-list', rooms[room.id].layout).append(html);
	rooms[room.id].dom.userList.nanoScroller();
}

function userAdd ( room, data ) {
	if(!$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data['nick'])+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout)[0]) {
		userFloorSend(room, userFloorMaker(data), data);
	}
}
function system(target, room, type, data) {
	if(type != 'notice' && type != 'toplayer') {
		data = text(data);
	}
	switch(type) {
		case 'invite':
			var result = $('<div>');
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideIndi) break;
			if(started_time >= new Date().getTime() - 1000)
				target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()+'">'+allot2(room.language.system[type], data)+'</div>');
			else {
				popup.confirm('개인채널 초대', data[0]+'님이 개인채널에 초대하였습니다. ', function(result) {
					if(result) {
						room.action.command('individual', data[2]);
					}
				});

				if("Notification" in window) {
					var options = {
						body : data[0]+'님이 개인채널에 초대하였습니다. '
					};
					var notification = new Notification("개인채널 초대", options);
					notification.onclick = function() {
						parent.focus();
						this.close();
					};

				}
			}
			break;
		case 'frozen':
			$(rooms[room.id].layout).addClass('frozen');
			target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()/1000+'">'+allot2(room.language.system[type], data)+'</div>');
			break;
		case 'defrozen':
			$(rooms[room.id].layout).removeClass('frozen');
			target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()/1000+'">'+allot2(room.language.system[type], data)+'</div>');
			break;
		case 'user_info':
			popup.alert('유저정보', allot2(room.language.system[type], data), function(pb, pu) {
			});
			break;
		case 'from_call':
			if(room.setting.data['sound.call'] && started_time < new Date().getTime() - 1000) {
				rooms[room.id].dom.content_target.append(sound('//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/sound/di_sound'));
			}
			
			if(started_time >= new Date().getTime() - 1000) {
				target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()/1000+'">'+allot2(room.language.system[type], data)+'</div>');
			} else {
				popup.alert('호출', allot2(room.language.system[type], data), function(pb, pu) {});
				if("Notification" in window) {
					var options = {
						body : allot2(room.language.system[type], data)
					};
					var notification = new Notification("호출", options);
					notification.onclick = function() {
						parent.focus();
						this.close();
					};
				}
			}
			
			break;
		case 'toplayer':
			var timeout = 0;
			if(data[4])
				timeout = data[4]*1000 - room.now();
			if(data[5] > 0 && (data[4] == 0 || (timeout > 0  && data[5]*1000 < timeout )))
				timeout = data[5]*1000;
			room.top_layer.add(allot2(room.language.system[type], data), data[1], data[2], timeout, data[6], data[7]);
			break;
		case 'changed_nick':
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideNickChange)
				return false;
		default:
			target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()/1000+'">'+allot2(room.language.system[type], data)+'</div>');
			break;
	}
	room.skin.scrollDown();
}

	//console.log('★★', room.setting.data);
	rooms[room.id] = this_room= {room:room, log : {}};

]오른쪽 <div class="room_setting" style="display:inline-block;"><img src="//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/black/setting.png" width="16" alt=""></div>를 클릭하여 채팅방 관리자 로그인 비밀번호를 설정해주세요.[
]관리자 로그인 비밀번호가 설정되어있지 않으면 채팅방에 아무도 없을때 모든 설정이 날라가고 새로운 접속자에게 권한이 넘어갑니다.[
]채팅방 관리자는 이 채팅방의 모든 권한을 가질 수 있습니다.[
]남에게 알려주지 마시고 쉬운 비밀번호로 설정하지 마세요.[
]관리자 로그인 비밀번호가 있더라도 2주동안 아무도 접속하지 않으면 채팅방이 자동 소멸됩니다.</div>';

	room.skin.window = window;

	room.skin.userMenu = new ( function userMenu_module() { 
		this.list = [];
		
		this.add = function( data ) {
			if(!data.id) return false;
			for(var i =0, l=this.list.length; i<l; i++) {
				if(this.list[i].id == data.id)
					return false;
			}
			data.layout = $('<div />').addClass('floor').text(data.text);
			this.list.push(data);
		}

		this.group = function( data1, data2 ) { 
			data1.layout = $('<div />').addClass('floor').text(data1.text);
			data2.layout = $('<div />').addClass('floor right').text(data2.text);

			this.list.push( [data1, data2] );
		}

		this.hr = function( data ) { 
			if(!data) data = {};
			data.id = 'hr';
			data.layout = $('<div class="hr"></div>');
			this.list.push(data);
		}

		this.remove = function( id ) {
			if(!id) return false;
			var i = this.list.length;
			while(i--) {
				if(isArray(this.list[i])) {
					if(this.list[i][1] && this.list[i][1].id == id)
						this.list[i].splice(1, 1);
					if(this.list[i][0] && this.list[i][0].id == id)
						this.list[i].splice(0, 1);
					if(this.list[i].length == 0)
						this.list.splice(i, 1);
				} else {
					if(this.list[i].id == id)
						this.list.splice(i, 1);
				}

			}
		}

		this.print = function ( target ) {
			var result = [];
			var self = this;
			for(var i = 0, l = this.list.length; i<l; i++) {
				if(isArray(this.list[i])) {
					var group_tmp = $('<div />').addClass('group');
					if(checkCondition(this.list[i][1], room, {target : target})) {
						result.push(onClick(this.list[i][1]));
					}
					if(checkCondition(this.list[i][0], room, {target : target})) {
						result.push(onClick(this.list[i][0]));
					}
					if(group_tmp.find('div').length > 0) {
						result.push(group_tmp);
					}

				} else {
					if(checkCondition(this.list[i], room, {target : target})) {
						result.push(onClick(this.list[i]));
					}
				}
			}
			return result;
		}

		function checkCondition( fn, room, data ) {
			if(fn && fn.condition && fn.condition(room, data) === false)
				return false;
			else
				return true;

		}

		function onClick(data) {
			if(!data) return ;
			return data.layout.click(function(e) {
				data.onClick && data.onClick( room,  {event:e, id:data.id, target:unescape($('#popupWrap').find('.subject').attr('nick'))});
			});
		}

	})();

	room.skin.menubar = new (function menubar_module() {
		this.list = [];
		this.menubar = $('.menuBar', rooms[room.id].layout);
		this.room = room;

		this.add = function(data) {
			if(!data.id) return false;

			for(var i = 0, l= this.list.length; i<l; i++){
				if (this.list[i].id == data.id) {
					return false;
				}
			}
			if(data.html) {
				data.layout = $(data.html);
			} else {
				data.layout = $('<div />');
			} 
			
			data.layout.attr('title', data.title || '').addClass('menu-style').addClass('menubar-'+data.id).on('change click', function(e) {
				data.event = e;
				data.onClick && data.onClick(room, data); 
			}).data('menuId', data.id); 
			if(data.icon)
				data.layout.css('backgroundImage', 'url('+data.icon+')');
			this.list.push(data);
			return true;
		}

		this.remove = function (id) {
			var i = this.list.length;
			while(i--) {
				if(this.list[i].id == id) {

					this.list[i].beforeUnload && this.list[i].beforeUnload();
					this.menubar.find('.menubar-'+i).remove();
					this.list[i].afterUnload && this.list[i].afterUnload();
					this.list.splice(i, 1);
				}
			}
			
			return true;
		}

		this.refresh = function () {
			var self = this;
			for(var i = 0, l= this.list.length; i<l; i++) {
				var data = this.list[i];
				if(this.menubar.find('.menubar-'+this.list[i].id).length > 0) {
					if(this.list[i].condition && this.list[i].condition( room, this.list[i] ) === false) { //삭제시작
						this.remove(data.id);
					}
				} else { 
					if(this.list[i].condition && this.list[i].condition( room, this.list[i] ) === false) { // 조건이 안됨
						continue;
					} else { 
						if(!this.list[i].beforeLoad || this.list[i].beforeLoad && this.list[i].beforeLoad(room, data) !== false) {
							this.menubar.append(this.list[i].layout);
							this.list[i].afterLoad && this.list[i].afterLoad(room, data);
						}
					}
				}
			}

			$(window).resize();
		}

		this.hide = function () {
			if(this.menubar.is(':visible')) {
				this.menubar.hide();
				$(window).resize();
			}
		}

		this.show  = function () {
			if(this.menubar.not(':visible')) {
				this.menubar.show();
				$(window).resize();
			}
		}

		this.toggle = function() {
			if(this.menubar.is(':visible'))
				this.hide();
			else
				this.show();
		}
		
	})();

	room.skin.menubar.add( { // 스크롤 등록
		id : 'scroll'
		, title : '스크롤 고정'
		, icon : '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/scroll.png'
		, beforeLoad : function( room, data ) {
			var self = this;
			data.layout.css({
				'backgroundPositionY' : '-4px'
				, 'float' : 'right'
				, 'margin' : 0
			});
			rooms[room.id].dom.content.find('.content').on("scroll", function(e){
				if(tooltip) tooltip.hide();
				if(rooms[room.id].log.temp_scroll_stop)
					return false;
				if ($(this).height() + this.scrollTop >= this.scrollHeight-30){
					$('.latest_chat', rooms[room.id].layout).hide();
					if (room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] !== 1) {
						room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] = 1;
					}
				} else {
					if (room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] === 1) {
						room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] = 0;
					}
				}
				self.refresh(room, data);
			});
			return true;
		}
		, onClick : function( room , data ) {
			if(room.setting.data['option.autoScroll']) {
				room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] = 0;
			} else {
				room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] = 1;
			}

			this.refresh(room, data);
		}
		, afterLoad : function( room, data ) {
		}
		, refresh : function( room, data ) { 
			if(room.setting.data['option.autoScroll']) { 
				data.layout.css("backgroundPositionX", '0');
			} else { 
				data.layout.css("backgroundPositionX", '100%');
			}
		}
	} );

	room.skin.menubar.add( { // bold 등록
		id : 'bold'
		, title : '굵게'
		, condition : function ( room, data ) { 
			if(!room.info['font']) return false;
		}
		, beforeLoad : function( room, data ) {
			var url = '';
			if(isWhiteness(room.skin.arguments.bottomBGColor))
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/black/bold.png';
			else
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/white/bold.png';

			var src = 'url('+url+')';
			data.layout.css('backgroundImage', src).addClass('hoverOpacity');
		}
		, onClick : function( room, data ) { 
			if(!data.layout.hasClass('on')) {
				data.layout.addClass('on');
				$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).css('fontWeight', 'bold');
				room.setting.data['style.bold'] = true;
			} else {
				data.layout.removeClass('on');
				$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).css('fontWeight', 'normal');
				room.setting.data['style.bold'] = false;
			}
			room.setting.save();
		}
		, afterLoad : function( room, data ) {
			if(room.setting.data['style.bold']) {
				$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).css('fontWeight', 'bold');
				data.layout.addClass('on');
			}
		}
		, afterUnload : function ( ) {
			$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).css('fontWeight', 'normal');
			room.setting.data['style.bold'] = false;
		}
	} );

	room.skin.menubar.add( { // 글씨색
	 	id : 'color'
		, title : '글씨색'
		, html : '<div><select name="colorpicker-picker-shortlist" class="colorpicker"></select></div>'
		, condition : function ( room, data ) { 
			if(!room.info['font']) return false;
		}
		, beforeLoad : function ( room, data ) { 
			var colorpicker = data.layout.find('.colorpicker');
			var colorList = ['#b71c1c', '#880E4F', '#4A148C', '#311B92', '#1A237E', '#0D47A1', '#01579B', '#006064', '#004D40', '#1B5E20', '#33691E', '#827717', '#F57F17', '#FF6F00', '#E65100', '#BF360C', '#3E2723', '#AB47BC', '#26C6DA', '#26A69A', '#E91E63', '#546E7A', '#BFA0ED'];
			if(room.skin.arguments.colorList) {
				colorList = room.skin.arguments.colorList.split(' ');
			}
			if(colorList.indexOf(room.skin.arguments.defaultColor || '#333333') == -1) {
				colorList.unshift(room.skin.arguments.defaultColor || '#333333');
			}
			for(var i = 0, len = colorList.length; i<len; i++ ) {
				colorpicker.append($('<option></option>').val(colorList[i]));
			}
			var color = room.setting.data['style.color'] || room.skin.arguments.defaultColor;
			colorpicker.val(color);
			$('.chatInput').css('color', color);
			room.setting.data['style.color'] = color;
			colorpicker.simplecolorpicker({picker: true});

		}
		, onClick : function ( room, data ) { 
		}
		, afterLoad : function ( room, data ) { 
			data.layout.on('change', function() {
				var color = data.layout.find('.colorpicker').val();
				$('.chatInput').css('color', color);
				room.setting.data['style.color'] = color;
				room.setting.save();
				var colorpicker = data.layout.find('.colorpicker');
				colorpicker.simplecolorpicker('hidePicker');;
			});
		}
	} );


	room.skin.menubar.add( { // emoticon  등록
		id : 'emoticon'
		, title : '이모티콘'
		, icon: ''
		, condition : function ( room, data ) { 
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) return false;
		}
		
		, REGEX_FOR_EMOTICON : new RegExp("\\<img[^>]*src\\=\\\"(https?:)?"+('//emoticon.inde.biz'.replace(/\//g, '\\/').replace(/\./g, '\\.'))+"\\/emoticon\\/([a-zA-Z_0-9]+)\\/(\\d+\\.(gif|jpe?g|png))\\\"[^>]*\\>", "gi")
		, toEmoticon : function(text) {
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) return false;
			if(text) { 
				text = text.replace(/\{e\|([a-zA-Z_0-9]+)\|(\d+\.(gif|jpe?g|png))\}/g, '<img src="//emoticon.inde.biz/emoticon/$1/$2">');
			}
			return text;
		}

		, fromEmoticon : function(text) {
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) return false;
			if(text) { 
				text = text.replace(this.REGEX_FOR_EMOTICON, '{e|$2|$3}');
			}
			return text;

		}

		, removeEmoticon : function(text) {
			if(text) { 
				text = text.replace(/\{e\|([a-zA-Z_0-9]+)\|(\d+\.(gif|jpe?g|png))\}/g, '');
				text = text.replace(this.REGEX_FOR_EMOTICON, '');
			}
			return text;
		}
		, beforeLoad : function( room, data ) {
			var url = '';
			if(isWhiteness(room.skin.arguments.bottomBGColor))
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/black/emoticon.png';
			else
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/white/emoticon.png';

			var src = 'url('+url+')';
			data.layout.css('backgroundImage', src).addClass('hoverOpacity');
			var self = this;
			$.fn.bindFirst = function(name, fn) {
    			// bind as you normally would
    			// don't want to miss out on any jQuery magic
    			this.on(name, fn);

    			// Thanks to a comment by @Martin, adding support for
    			// namespaced events too.
    			this.each(function() {
        			var handlers = $._data(this, 'events')[name.split('.')[0]];
        			// take out the handler we just inserted from the end
        			var handler = handlers.pop();
        			// move it at the beginning
        			handlers.splice(0, 0, handler);
    			});
			};
			$('.chatInput').bindFirst('keydown', function(e) { 
				if(e.keyCode == 13 ) {
					$(this).html(self.fromEmoticon($(this).html()));
				}
			});
			room.on('after.message', function(room, data) {
				var target = $('.content div:last-child .chatContent', room.skin.document);
				var target2 = room.skin.dom.latest_chat.find('.chatContent');

				if(!room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) {
					target.html(self.toEmoticon(target.html()));
					target2.html(self.toEmoticon(target2.html()));
				} else
					target.html(self.removeEmoticon(target.html()));

				room.skin.scrollDown();
			});
			room.on('after.whisper', function(room, data) {
				var target = $('.content div:last-child .chatContent', room.skin.document);
				if(!room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) {
					target.html(self.toEmoticon(target.html()));
				} else
					target.html(self.removeEmoticon(target.html()));
				room.skin.scrollDown();
			});
		}
		, onClick : function( room, data ) { 
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideEmoticon) return false;
			popup.add($('#emoticon_popup').html(), 'emoticon_popup', function(layer, pb, pu) {
				/*
				pu.find('input:first').focus();
				pu.find(".nickname").val(room.my.nick);
				*/

				var x = data.event.pageX;
				var y = data.event.pageY;

				/* ie7 에서 wrap 의 넓이가 안정해지면 자식객체가 width 를 100% 으로 써버림 (float:right 하는순간 width 100%)
				if(pu.outerWidth() < 120)
					pu.width(120);
					*/
				pu.width($('body').width() < 200? $('body').width():200);
				if( x < 0 )
					x = 0;
				if( x > $('body').width() - pu.outerWidth())
					x = $('body').width() - pu.outerWidth();
				if( y > $('body').height() - pu.outerHeight())
					y = $('body').height() - pu.outerHeight();
				pu.css("top", y).css("left", x);
				
				var html = '';

				for(var i =1; i <= 127; i++) {
					html += '<img src="//emoticon.inde.biz/emoticon/onionhead/'+leadingZeros(i, 3)+'.gif" code="onionhead|'+leadingZeros(i, 3)+'.gif">';
				}

				pu.find('.emoticon_middle').html(html);
				pb.on('click', function() {
					layer.close();
				});
				pu.on('click', 'img', function() {
					$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).append('<img src="'+$(this).attr('src')+'">');
					var el = $('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout)[0];
					el.focus();
					if (typeof window.getSelection != "undefined"
							&& typeof document.createRange != "undefined") {
						var range = document.createRange();
						range.selectNodeContents(el);
						range.collapse(false);
						var sel = window.getSelection();
						sel.removeAllRanges();
						sel.addRange(range);
					} else if (typeof document.body.createTextRange != "undefined") {
						var textRange = document.body.createTextRange();
						textRange.moveToElementText(el);
						textRange.collapse(false);
						textRange.select();
					}
					rooms[room.id].textarea_reload();
					layer.close();

				});
				/*
				pu.one('click', '.ok', function() {
					//alert('오케이');
					commandSwitch(room, ['nick', pu.find(".nickname").val() ]);
					layer.close();
					hideSetting();
				}).one('click', '.cancel', function() {
					//alert('거절');
					layer.close();
					hideSetting();
				});
				*/
			});
		}
	} );

		
	room.skin.menubar.add( { // 사진 업로드 등록
		id : 'picture'
		, title : '업로드'
		, html : '<div><form action="//sexbam.inde.biz/s/index" method="post" target="hiddenImageUpload" enctype="multipart/form-data"><input type="hidden" name="referer" /><input type="hidden" name="room" value="uchat_main" /><input type="hidden" name="target" value="" /><img><input type="file" id="uploads" name="uploads" class="uploads" style="position: absolute; z-index: 19999; top: -1000px; left: -1000px;" /></form></div>'
		, condition : function ( room, data ) { 
			if(room.skin.arguments.hideUpload) return false;
		}
		, beforeLoad : function( room, data ) {
			var url = '';
			var hidden = document.createElement('iframe');
			hidden.name = hidden.id = 'hiddenImageUpload';
			$('body').append($(hidden).width(0).height(0));

			if(isWhiteness(room.skin.arguments.bottomBGColor))
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/black/picture.png';
			else
				url = '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/white/picture.png';

			//data.layout.css('backgroundImage', src).addClass('hoverOpacity');
			data.layout.find('img').attr('src', url).css({height:'100%', width:'100%', zIndex:10}).click(function() {
				$(this).closest('form').find('input[type=file]').click();
			});;
			
			var $data = data;
			XD.receiveMessage(function(data) {
				var upload_json = JSONParse(data.data);
				if(upload_json.status) {
					$('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout).append(upload_json.url);
					placeCaretAtEnd($('.chatInput', rooms[room.id].layout)[0]);
					$data.layout.find('.uploads').prop('value', '');
				} else
					alert(upload_json.msg);
			}, location.protocol+'//sexbam.inde.biz');

			data.layout.find('.uploads').on('change', function(e) {
    			var count=1;

    			var files = e.currentTarget.files; // puts all files into an array
    			// call them as such; files[0].size will get you the file size of the 0th file

    			if(!files.length)
    				return false;

    			for (var x in files) {
        			var filesize = ((files[x].size/1024)/1024).toFixed(4); // MB
        			if (files[x].name != "item" && typeof files[x].name != "undefined") { 
        				var ext = files[x].name.split('.').pop();
        				if(indexOf(['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif'], ext.toLowerCase()) == -1) {
        					alert("그림파일만 허용하고 있습니다.");
        					return false;
        				}
        				if(filesize >= 3) {
        					alert("파일 크기가 3MB를 넘습니다.");
        					return false;
        				}
        			}
    			}
				data.layout.find('[name=referer]').val(location.href);
				data.layout.find('form').submit();
			});

		}
	} );
	
	room.skin.menubar.add( {  // 어드민 콜
		id : 'call_admin'
		, title : '관리자 호출'
		, icon : '//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/alarm.png'
		, condition : function( room, data ) {
			if(!room.info['call_admin'])
				return false;
		}
		, onClick : function( room, data ) {
			commandSwitch(room, ['call_admin']);
		}
	} );

	

	var content_target = $('.content', rooms[room.id].layout).not(".scroll-wrapper");
	rooms[room.id].dom.content_target = content_target;

	room._on("system", function ( room, data ) {
		system(content_target, room, data.type, data.data);
	});
	room._on('update', function ( room, data ) {
		// 여기에 업데이트시에 갱신해야되는거 넣어야됨
	});
	room._on("join", function( room, data ) {
		// refresh skin menubar
		room.skin.menubar.refresh();
		content_target.append('<div class="line system" data-tiptext="{ago}" created="'+Uchat.getServerSecond()/1000+'">'+text(room.info.name)+' 연결 완료</div>');
		started_time = new Date().getTime();
		$('.chatname', rooms[room.id].layout).text(room.info.name);

		$('.count', rooms[room.id].layout).text('0');

		$('.login, .room_setting', rooms[room.id].layout).hide();

		if(room.my.auth < 2 && ( room.info.mode == MODE_CHANNEL || !room.info['userLinkage'] ) )
			$('.login', rooms[room.id].layout).show();
		if(room.my.auth == 3 && room.info.mode !== MODE_INDI)
			$('.room_setting', rooms[room.id].layout).show();
		rooms[room.id].userListDom.init();
			
		!room.skin.arguments.hideChatRecord && room.action.command('chatList');
		room.action.command('noticeList');

	});
	
	room._on("whisper", function( room, data ) {
		var myClass = '';
		var myNick = room.my.nick;
		if(data['from']['nick'] != myNick && data['to']['nick'] == myNick)
			rooms[room.id].log.last_whisper = data['from']['nick'];
		if(data['from']['nick'] == myNick)
			myClass = ' myLine';
		var html = '';
		var to_icon_set = icons_parsing(data['to']['icons']);
		var from_icon_set = icons_parsing(data['from']['icons']);

		html += '<div class="line'+myClass+'" title="'+data['created']+'">';
		html += '<span class="whisperFlag">[귓]</span>';
		if (data['from']['nick'] == myNick) {
			html += to_icon_set[0];
			html += '<span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data['to']['nick'])+'" uid="'+data['to']['id']+'">'+text(data['to']['nick'])+' </span> 님에게';
			html += to_icon_set[1];
		} else if(data['to']['nick'] == myNick) {
			html += from_icon_set[0];
			html += '<span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data['from']['nick'])+'" uid="'+data['from']['id']+'">'+text(data['from']['nick'])+'</span> 님이';
			html += from_icon_set[1];
		} else {
			html += from_icon_set[0];
			html += '<span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data['from']['nick'])+'" uid="'+data['from']['id']+'">'+text(data['from']['nick'])+'</span>';
			html += from_icon_set[1];
			html += ' -> ';
			html += to_icon_set[0];
			html += '<span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data['to']['nick'])+'" uid="'+data['to']['id']+'">'+text(data['to']['nick'])+' </span>';
			html += to_icon_set[1];

		}
		html += '&nbsp;:&nbsp;';
		html += '<span class="chatContent">'+linkify(text(data['content']))+'</span></div>';
		content_target.append(html);
		room.skin.scrollDown();
	});
	room._on("message", function( room, data ) {
		var myClass = '';
		if(data.user['nick'] == room.my.nick)
			myClass = ' myLine';
		var style = [];
		if(data['style']['bold'])
			style.push('font-weight: bold;');
		if(data['style']['italic'])
			style.push('font-style: italic;');
		if(data['style']['underline'])
			style.push('text-decoration: underline;');
		if(data['style']['color'])
			style.push('color: '+data['style']['color']+';');
		if(data['style']['size'])
			style.push('font-size: '+(room.skin.arguments.fontSize||data['style']['size'])+';');
		var html = '<div class="line'+myClass+'" data-tiptext="'+escape(data.user['nick'])+' - {ago}" created="'+data['time']+'">';
		var icons_set = icons_parsing(data.user['icons']);
			
		if(data.user['nickcon']) {
			var nickcon = imageMaker(data.user['nickcon']);
		}


		html += icons_set[0]+'<span class="nick'+(myClass?' myNick':'')+'" nick="'+escape(data.user['nick'])+'">'+(nickcon?nickcon:text(data.user['nick']))+icons_set[1]+':</span>&nbsp;<span class="chatContent" style="'+style.join(' ')+'">'+linkify(text(data['content']))+'</span></div>';
		content_target.append(html);
		if((room.setting.data['option.autoScroll'] === 0 || rooms[room.id].log.temp_scroll_stop) && rooms[room.id].dom.content_target.height() != rooms[room.id].dom.content_target[0].scrollHeight)
			$('.latest_chat .latest_chat_content', rooms[room.id].layout).html(html).parent().show();
		room.skin.scrollDown();
	});
	room._on("user.modi", function( room, data ) {
		//console.log(target, change_data);
		var targetData = room.user.get(data.target);
		for(var i in data.changed) {
			switch(i) {
				case 'nick':	
					$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data.target)+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout).attr('nick', escape(data.changed['nick'])).find('span').text(data.changed['nick']);
					system(content_target, room, "changed_nick", [data.target, data.changed['nick']]);
					break;
				case 'auth':
					if(targetData) {
						$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data.target)+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout).remove();

						userFloorSend(room, userFloorMaker(targetData), targetData);
					}
					if(room.my.nick == data.target) {
						$('.login, .room_setting', rooms[room.id].layout).hide();
						if(room.my.auth < 2 && room.info.mode == MODE_CHANNEL)
							$('.login', rooms[room.id].layout).show();
						if(room.my.auth == 3)
							$('.room_setting', rooms[room.id].layout).show();
					}
					break;
				case 'mute':
					if(targetData['mute'])
						$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data.target)+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout).addClass('mute')
					else
						$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data.target)+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout).removeClass('mute')
					break;
				default:
					break;
			}
		}
	});
	room._on("user.list", function( room, data ) {
		var list = [[],[],[],[],[]]; 
		for(var i = 0, len=data.list.length; i<len; i++) {
			//data.list[i]['connected'] = timeSince(data.list[i]['connected']+'000');
			//userAdd( rooms[room.id], data.list[i] );
			if(room.my.nick != data.list[i]['nick'])
				list[data.list[i]['auth']].push(userFloorMaker(data.list[i]));
			else {
				list[4].push(userFloorMaker(data.list[i]));
			}
		}
		rooms[room.id].dom.userList.find('.userList').children('div').html('')
		for(var i =0, len=list.length; i<len; i++) {
			if(i==4) {
				userFloorSend(room, list[i].join(''), {nick:room.my.nick});
			}else
				userFloorSend(room, list[i].join(''), {auth:i}); 
		}
		$('.count', rooms[room.id].layout).html($('.userFloor', rooms[room.id].layout).length);
	});
	room._on("user.join", function( room, data ) {
		userAdd( room, data.user );
		if(room.setting.data['access.joinout']) {
			content_target.append('<div class="line system" title="'+data.user['connected']+'"><span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data.user['nick'])+'">'+text(data.user['nick'])+'</span>님 입장.</div>');
			room.skin.scrollDown();
		}
		$('.count', rooms[room.id].layout).html($('.userFloor', rooms[room.id].layout).length);
	});
	room._on("user.quit", function( room, data ) {
		$('.userFloor[nick="'+escape(data.user['nick'])+'"]', rooms[room.id].layout).remove();
		if(room.setting.data['access.joinout']) {
			content_target.append('<div class="line system" title="'+room.getTimeStamp()+'"><span class="nick" nick="'+escape(data.user['nick'])+'">'+text(data.user['nick'])+'</span>님 퇴장.</div>');
			room.skin.scrollDown();
		}
		$('.count', rooms[room.id].layout).html($('.userFloor', rooms[room.id].layout).length);
		
	});
	room._on("user.count", function ( room, data ) {
		room.count = data.count;
		$('.count', rooms[room.id].layout).html(data.count);
	});
	room._on("error", function ( room, data ) {
		switch(data.code) {
			case 418:
				$(rooms[room.id].layout).addClass('frozen');			
				break;
		}
		if(data.code > 700) {
			switch(data.code) {
				case 701:
					popup.password('접속 비밀번호', room.language.error[data.code], '', function(result) {
						room.action.command('password', result);
					});
					break;
				default:
					break;
			}
		} else
			content_target.append('<div class="line system" title="'+room.getTimeStamp()+'">'+room.language.error[data.code]+'</div>');
		room.skin.scrollDown();
	});
	room._on("control", function( room, data ) {
		switch(data.type) {
			case 'clearLog':
				$('.content', rooms[room.id].layout).html('');
				room.skin.scrollDown();
				break;
			case 'ad':
				rooms[room.id].dom.top.find('.logo').html('<img src="//sexbam.1.inde.biz/skin/basic/img/logo.gif" style="height:100%;">');
				if(!rooms[room.id].dom.menubar.find('.icon_logo').length)
					rooms[room.id].dom.menubar.append($($('#uchatLogo').html()).addClass('menu-style').click(function() { 
						window.open('http://uchat.io', '_blank');
					}));
				$(rooms[room.id].layout).on('click', '.logo', function() {
					window.open('http://uchat.io', '_blank');
				});
				$('.onlyAd').show();
				break;
		}
	});
	room._on("externalEvent", function( room, data ) {
		if( type == 'click' ) {
			popup.closeByType('userMenu');
		}
	});
	room._on("disconnect", function( room, data) {
		content_target.append('<div class="line system" title="'+room.getTimeStamp()+'">서버 연결 끊김</div>');
		room.skin.scrollDown();
	});
});

if (!Array.prototype.indexOf) {
	Array.prototype.indexOf = function (searchElement, fromIndex) {
		if ( this === undefined || this === null ) {
			throw new TypeError( '"this" is null or not defined' );
		}

		var length = this.length >>> 0; // Hack to convert object.length to a UInt32

		fromIndex = +fromIndex || 0;

		if (Math.abs(fromIndex) === Infinity) {
			fromIndex = 0;
		}

		if (fromIndex < 0) {
			fromIndex += length;
			if (fromIndex < 0) {
				fromIndex = 0;
			}
		}

		for (;fromIndex < length; fromIndex++) {
			if (this[fromIndex] === searchElement) {
				return fromIndex;
			}
		}

		return -1;
	};
}


function check_audio_tag () {
	var a = document.createElement('audio');
	return !!(a.canPlayType && a.canPlayType('audio/mpeg;').replace(/no/, ''));
}

function escapeHTML (data) {
    if(isArray(data)) {
        for(var i = 0, limit = data.length; i<limit; i++ ) {
            if(isStr(data[i]))
                data[i] = escapeHTML(data[i]);
        }
        return data;
    } else if(isStr(data)) {
		return data.replace(/&/gi, '&amp;').replace(/</gi, "&lt;").replace(/"/gi, "&quot;");
    } else {
    	return data;
    }
}


function unescapeHTML(html) {
    forEscapeHTMLDom.innerHTML = html;
    return forEscapeHTMLDom.textContent;
}

function isArray (source) {
    return Object.prototype.toString.call(source) === '[object Array]';
}

function isJson (source) {
	return source && source.constructor === {}.constructor;
}

function isStr (source) {
    return source && source.constructor === ''.constructor;
}


function linkify(text){
    if (text) {
        text = text.replace(
            /(((((http|ftp|https):)?\/\/)|(www\.))[\w\-_]+(\.[\w\-_]+)+([\wㄱ-ㅎㅏ-ㅣ가-힣\;\-\.,@?^=%&:/~\+#]*[\w\-\@?^=%&/~\+#])?)/gi,
            function(url){
                var full_url = url;
                if (!full_url.match('^(https?:)?\/\/')) {
                    full_url = '//' + full_url;
                }
                return '<a href="' + full_url + '" target="_blank">' + url + '</a>';
            }
        );
    }
    return text;
}


function leadingZeros(n, digits) {
	var zero = '';
	n = n.toString();
	if (n.length < digits) {
		for (var i = 0; i < digits - n.length; i++)
		zero += '0';
	}
	return zero + n;
}



function strip(html)
{
   var tmp = document.createElement("DIV");
   tmp.innerHTML = html;
   return tmp.textContent || tmp.innerText || "";
}

function sound(src) {
	var result;
	if(started_time >= new Date().getTime() - 1000) return false;
	if(check_audio_tag()) {
		result = '<audio autoplay="autoplay"><source src="'+src+'.mp3" type="audio/mpeg"><embed hidden="true" autostart="true" loop="false" src="'+src+'.mp3" /></audio>';
	} else {
		result = '<object type="application/x-shockwave-flash" data="'+src+'.swf" style="width:20px; height:10px;"><param name="movie" value="'+src+'.swf" /></object>';
	}
	return result
}

function isWhiteness(bgColor) {
	var color = (bgColor.charAt(0) === '#') ? bgColor.substring(1, 7) : (bgColor.charAt(0) === 'r') ? rgb2hex(bgColor).substring(1, 7) : bgColor;
	var r = parseInt(color.substring(0, 2), 16); // hexToR
	var g = parseInt(color.substring(2, 4), 16); // hexToG
	var b = parseInt(color.substring(4, 6), 16); // hexToB
	var uicolors = [r / 255, g / 255, b / 255];
	var c = [];
	for(var col in uicolors) {
		if (col <= 0.03928) {
			c.push(uicolors[col] / 12.92);
		} else {
			c.push(Math.pow((uicolors[col] + 0.055) / 1.055, 2.4));
		}
	}
	var L = (0.2126 * c[0]) + (0.7152 * c[1]) + (0.0722 * c[2]);
	return (L > 0.179) ? 1 : 0; // 1 = font color black, 0 = font color white
}

function rgb2hex(rgb) {
    rgb = rgb.match(/^rgba?\(\s*(\d+),\s*(\d+),\s*(\d+)(,\s*\d+)?\)$/);
    function hex(x) {
        return ("0" + parseInt(x).toString(16)).slice(-2);
    }
    return "#" + hex(rgb[1]) + hex(rgb[2]) + hex(rgb[3]);
}

function placeCaretAtEnd(el) {
    el.focus();
    if (typeof window.getSelection != "undefined"
            && typeof document.createRange != "undefined") {
        var range = document.createRange();
        range.selectNodeContents(el);
        range.collapse(false);
        var sel = window.getSelection();
        sel.removeAllRanges();
        sel.addRange(range);
    } else if (typeof document.body.createTextRange != "undefined") {
        var textRange = document.body.createTextRange();
        textRange.moveToElementText(el);
        textRange.collapse(false);
        textRange.select();
    }
}
function timeSince(now, date) {
  	var seconds = Math.floor((now - date) / 1000);
  	var interval = Math.floor(seconds / 31536000);
  	if (interval > 1) {
    	return interval + "년 전";
  	}
  	interval = Math.floor(seconds / 2592000);
  	if (interval > 1) {
    	return interval + "개월 전";
  	}
  	interval = Math.floor(seconds / 86400);
  	if (interval > 1) {
    	return interval + "일 전";
  	}
  	interval = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);
  	if (interval > 1) {
    	return interval + "시간 전";
  	}
  	interval = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
  	if (interval > 1) {
    	return interval + "분 전";
  	}

  	interval = Math.floor(seconds / 20);
  	if (interval == 0  || seconds < 0) {
  		return '방금 전'
  	}
  	return Math.floor(seconds) + "초 전";
}
function shadeColor2(color, percent) {   
    var f=parseInt(color.slice(1),16),t=percent<0?0:255,p=percent<0?percent*-1:percent,R=f>>16,G=f>>8&0x00FF,B=f&0x0000FF;
    return "#"+(0x1000000+(Math.round((t-R)*p)+R)*0x10000+(Math.round((t-G)*p)+G)*0x100+(Math.round((t-B)*p)+B)).toString(16).slice(1);
}
